<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderin.html>onderin</a> (24836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderin.html>onderin</a></strong>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderlopen.html>onderlopen</a></strong>

<ol><li>to become flooded</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderneming.html>onderneming</a> (6901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondernemen.html>ondernemen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">undertake</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderneming.html>onderneming</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondernemingen.html>ondernemingen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderneminkje.html>onderneminkje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to distinguish, to discriminate
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:goed.html>Goed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kwaad.html>kwaad</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunnen.html>kunnen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:onderscheiden.html>onderscheiden</a></b>.</i>

***ondertiteling.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>ondertiteling</a> (11137)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ondertitelen</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ing</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>ondertiteling</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>ondertitelingen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:subtitles.html>subtitles</a> to a video in a particular language <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">see usage note</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; sub.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>ondertiteling</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>deze</a> actiefilm <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedroevend.html>bedroevend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slecht.html>slecht</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:subtitles.html>subtitles</a></b> of this action <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> agonisingly bad.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:documentaire.html>documentaire</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heeft.html>heeft</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>ondertitelingen</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:negen.html>negen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:talen.html>talen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The documentary <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:subtitles.html>subtitles</a></b> in nine languages.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>Ondertiteling</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often used collectively for all the <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> textual versions of the dialogue of one <a href = vnd.unilang:film.html>film</a> in one language; the plural <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> often used in reference to versions in multiple languages or multiple <a href = vnd.unilang:films.html>films</a>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertiteling.html>ondertiteling</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tussen.html>tussen</a></i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertussen.html>ondertussen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>meanwhile, in the meantime</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ondertussen.html>Ondertussen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes incorrectly <a href = vnd.unilang:claimed.html>claimed</a> to be a false contamination of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:intussen.html>intussen</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onderwijl.html>onderwijl</a></i>, but its usage dates back to at least 1548. In contrast, the earliest mention of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:intussen.html>intussen</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> from 1722.
